🥔 VegToon Studio📐 Math🎙️ Model🔒 CharactersFull ScriptShotsTitles & Thumbs📖 STORY 12

← Veg-Toon Studio / Script

STORY 12of 12
🎤 DIALOGUE-LED (hybrid) · 16 beats · 58 self-contained 8s shots · ~10:04–12:07 min · runaway-bride wedding drama · NEW photoreal veg-head-on-human style

😭 गरीब आलू को ठुकराकर अमीर लहसुन से शादी 💔 फिर जयमाला पर चमत्कार | Sabji Cartoon | Hindi Kahani

A humble tiffin-delivery man loves a rich man’s daughter. A scheming aunt and a fake “London-return” millionaire tear them apart — until, at the jaimala itself, a little cousin’s phone recording burns the lie down and the bride runs. First script in the NEW photoreal veg-head-on-human-body style, and the first built dialogue-first.

🆕 What’s new in Story 12 — (1) DIALOGUE-LED: 59% of spoken words are character dialogue, 41% narrator (Story 11 was 77% narrator). Verified against the niche: 7 of 9 sampled mega-hits are dialogue-dominant. (2) HYBRID VOICES: 10 spotlight lines are Veo3-native lip-synced 🎤; all other lines ride the external voice track 🎧 over held scenes with mouths closed — exactly how the 1M+ rivals ship dialogue. (3) 8-SECOND clips — the real Veo 3.1 cap (old “~8–10s” pacing is retired; hold a clip’s tail frame in the edit where audio overruns). (4) NEW ART STYLE: photoreal vegetable head on a human body in Indian dress — the confirmed current winning look. Stories 1–11 keep the old cute full-veg style; do NOT re-render them.

📐 Length math

Runtime = spoken words ÷ Hindi pace (audio leads; clips are held/frozen on their tail frame in the edit wherever the track overruns 8s). All numbers computed from the script below.

1309
spoken words
58
shots (8s each)
41/59
% narration / dialogue
~10:04–12:07
min at natural pace

Narration 542 words · dialogue 767 words across 66 lines (10 of them 🎤 Veo3 lip-synced, the rest 🎧 voice-track) · visual floor 58×8s = 7:44 before edit holds. Sits inside the verified breakout band (8:28–13:32, median ≈9:20 — July 2026 pull).

🎙️ How to produce it (hybrid model)

  1. STEP 0 — VALIDATION PASS (do this before anything else): render the 7 canonical character portraits from the Character section, then ONE test dialogue clip (use Shot 4.4 — Aloo’s इज़्ज़त line). Check: no mask/second-head artifacts at the collar, no potato→rock / carrot→radish drift, Hindi lip-sync lands on the veg mouth, and no refusal on the wedding beats. Only then batch the rest. If a portrait drifts, fix its wording once — every prompt reuses the same lock verbatim.
  2. For each shot: generate the still from its IMAGE prompt (2–3 takes, pick the clean one), then feed the still + its VIDEO prompt to Veo3 for one 8-second clip. Every prompt is standalone — full character locks are embedded inside it.
  3. 🎤 Lip-sync shots (10 of them): the VIDEO prompt embeds the exact Hindi line, speaker, voice tone and lip-sync instruction — Veo3 voices that line natively. Budget extra takes for wrong-mouth failures; the line must end by ~7s.
  4. 🎧 Voice-track shots (all other dialogue + all narration): the clip is rendered with mouths closed/neutral; the lines are recorded on the external voice track and laid over in the edit. Where the audio for a scene overruns its 8s clip, hold or slow the clip’s tail frame — this is exactly how every 1M+ rival ships dialogue, and the audience demonstrably doesn’t care about lip-sync.
  5. Record the voice track from the Full Script (~110–120 wpm) — 4 voices cover the whole cast (doubling map in the Character section) plus the narrator. One session, one consistent voice per character for the whole video.
  6. Group/wedding scenes are the drift hotspot (many locks in one prompt): plan extra takes there. If using Flow’s Ingredients-to-Video, cite at most the 3 canonical portraits of the most prominent characters in that frame — the text locks cover the rest.
  7. Edit: shot number = play order (1.1 plays first) — assemble in order, no re-shuffling. BGM from YouTube Audio Library / Pixabay only (never NCS). Add the Hindi thumbnail overlay in Canva, never in the AI render.

🔒 Character Lock — new photoreal hybrid cast

Story 12 debuts the veg-head-on-human-body style. These exact blocks are baked verbatim into every image and video prompt below — this sheet is for reference and for rendering the 7 canonical portraits (Step 0).

CHARACTER LOCK · full cast (also embedded in every prompt)
ALOO, the humble tiffin-delivery hero — a photorealistic young man whose entire head IS a single large raw POTATO (must be a real aloo/potato). HEAD SHAPE & SKIN: a lumpy oval tuber slightly larger than a human head, matte earthy tan-brown skin with fine dimples, shallow potato eyes and a few faint soil freckles, dry matte texture, never shiny. FACE NOW: neutral, calm; warm brown eyes and a gentle mouth formed naturally in the potato skin. BODY & DRESS: a normal adult human body with ordinary human hands, wearing a simple off-white cotton kurta over worn dark jeans, a faded red-checked gamcha around his neck. DO NOT: his head is NOT a rock, NOT a coconut, NOT a smooth brown ball — a real dimpled potato; not orange, no leafy top, never shiny.

GAJAR, the warm-hearted heroine — a photorealistic young woman whose entire head IS a single fresh CARROT (must be a real gajar/carrot). HEAD SHAPE & SKIN: a tapering conical bright red-orange carrot with fine ridge rings across the surface, and a lush crown of feathery green carrot fronds flowing back from the top like hair. FACE NOW: neutral, calm; bright kind eyes and a soft mouth formed naturally in the carrot skin, a rosy glow on the cheeks. BODY & DRESS: a normal adult human body with ordinary human hands, wearing a neat mustard-yellow office kurti with a teal dupatta and a slim office ID lanyard. DO NOT: she is NOT a radish and NOT a mooli — never white, cream or pink, never a rounded bulb; and NOT a tomato and NOT a red chilli — her head stays bright red-ORANGE with its fine ridge rings, never the deep red of her clothing; keep the red-orange taper and the green frond crown always visible, even through a sheer dupatta.

BAINGAN SETH, Gajar's rich status-proud father — a photorealistic older man whose entire head IS a single large glossy deep-purple BRINJAL/EGGPLANT (must be a real baingan) with its green calyx cap sitting on top like short hair. HEAD SHAPE & SKIN: a heavy teardrop eggplant, deep aubergine-purple, glossy waxed sheen, the green star calyx always visible on the crown. FACE NOW: neutral, calm; deep-set hooded eyes and a heavy mouth formed naturally in the brinjal skin, a grey moustache ridge. BODY & DRESS: a normal adult human body with ordinary human hands, wearing a rich cream silk kurta under a gold-buttoned bandhgala waistcoat, a thick gold wristwatch, heavy gold rings, a polished gold-topped cane. DO NOT: his head is NOT a plum, NOT a purple balloon, NOT an onion; the green calyx cap must stay; body heavyset, never slim.

PYAZ AUNTY, the scheming aunt — a photorealistic middle-aged woman whose entire head IS a single reddish-purple ONION (must be a real pyaz) with glossy papery skin, clearly visible concentric layer lines, a small dry sprout-tuft at the crown pulled back like a tight bun, and a wisp of papery skin peeling at one temple. FACE NOW: neutral, calm; narrow calculating eyes and a thin honeyed smile formed naturally in the onion skin. BODY & DRESS: a normal adult human body with ordinary human hands, wearing a sharp magenta-and-gold silk saree draped tightly, heavy gold jhumka earrings, a small designer clutch. DO NOT: her head is NOT an apple, NOT a tomato, NOT a plain purple ball; the papery concentric layer lines must stay visible.

LEHSUN, the fraud "London-return" groom — a photorealistic slick young man whose entire head IS a single cream-white GARLIC bulb (must be a real lehsun) with distinct vertical clove ridges, a papery satin sheen, and a short dry stem-tip on the crown combed like a puff of hair. FACE NOW: neutral, calm; expressive half-lidded eyes and a mobile mouth formed naturally in the garlic skin. BODY & DRESS: a normal adult human body with ordinary human hands, wearing a fitted navy designer blazer over a printed silk shirt, thick stacked gold chains, a flashy gold watch, designer sunglasses hooked at the collar. DO NOT: his head is NOT an onion — no purple, no reddish tint, no concentric rings; the vertical white clove segments must stay visible; never in purple cloth.

TAMATAR, Aloo's loyal friend and fellow rider — a photorealistic young man whose entire head IS a single glossy bright-red TOMATO (must be a real tamatar) with a small green star calyx and stem on top, plump smooth skin with a soft sheen. FACE NOW: neutral, calm; big soft honest eyes that well up easily and a wide warm mouth formed naturally in the tomato skin. BODY & DRESS: a normal adult human body with ordinary human hands, wearing a faded yellow t-shirt under a grey delivery vest, dark trousers, a phone in a chest pocket. DO NOT: his head is NOT an apple, NOT an onion, NOT a capsicum; keep the green star calyx and the plump round red shape.

MOOLI, Gajar's sharp young cousin, the underestimated ally — a photorealistic young woman, late teens, whose entire head IS a single fresh white DAIKON RADISH (must be a real mooli), smooth cream-white with a faint waxy sheen, and a perky bunch of green radish leaves sprouting from the crown tied like a high ponytail. FACE NOW: neutral, calm; quick bright determined eyes and a resolute little mouth formed naturally in the radish skin. BODY & DRESS: a normal adult human body with ordinary human hands, wearing a simple lavender salwar-kameez with a small cross-body phone pouch. DO NOT: she is NOT a carrot — never orange, never red, never tapering-ridged; keep her smooth white body and the green leaf ponytail.

🧑‍🎨 Canonical portrait prompts — render & approve these FIRST

PORTRAIT — ALOO (आलू)
CAMERA: front-facing medium close-up, eye-level, 50mm lens look, neutral standing pose, plain warm grey studio background. SUBJECT — CHARACTER LOCK: ALOO, the humble tiffin-delivery hero — a photorealistic young man whose entire head IS a single large raw POTATO (must be a real aloo/potato). HEAD SHAPE & SKIN: a lumpy oval tuber slightly larger than a human head, matte earthy tan-brown skin with fine dimples, shallow potato eyes and a few faint soil freckles, dry matte texture, never shiny. FACE NOW: calm, friendly, looking straight at the camera; warm brown eyes and a gentle mouth formed naturally in the potato skin. BODY & DRESS: a normal adult human body with ordinary human hands, wearing a simple off-white cotton kurta over worn dark jeans, a faded red-checked gamcha around his neck, a scuffed grey-blue delivery windbreaker with a boxy insulated delivery bag slung on his shoulder. DO NOT: his head is NOT a rock, NOT a coconut, NOT a smooth brown ball — a real dimpled potato; not orange, no leafy top, never shiny. Photorealistic cinematic 3D render in the Indian drama-film look: real-world Indian settings, natural volumetric light, shallow depth of field, rich warm cinematic grade, 16:9 widescreen, high detail. Every character is a photorealistic figure whose entire head IS a single real vegetable — a vegetable head resting naturally on the collar of a normal adult human body in Indian dress, with ordinary human hands and human proportions, no visible seam at the neck; the facial features are formed naturally in the vegetable's own skin, expressive and human-like, brows suggested by soft ridges. NEVER a mask, NEVER a costume, NEVER a human face, human skin-tone head or human hair anywhere. LIGHTING: soft even key light with a gentle warm rim. NEGATIVE: no morphing, no warping, no melting, no smooth featureless blob, no color-shift, no species swap, no mask or helmet look, no visible neck seam, no human face or human hair, no extra limbs, no distorted hands; absolutely NO text, letters, numbers, captions, subtitles, watermark or logo anywhere; no floating dust, sand or airborne particles.

🎧 Voice cast — 4 voices + narrator cover everything

VoicePlaysDirection
M1 · deep older maleBaingan Seth · guards · recovery agentsarrogant boom early → broken and soft after the exposé
M2 · young maleAloo · Tamatar (brighter, faster) · Lehsun (oily polish, shrill in panic)three registers of one voice — sincere / warm-cracking / fake-refined
F1 · young femaleGajar · Mooli (quicker, lighter)warm and breaking at peaks / fearless and clear
F2 · mid femalePyaz Aunty · phone operatorhoney over a blade
N · narratorthe storyteller (same voice as previous videos)~110–120 wpm, short bridges only — dialogue carries this story

📜 Full Script — the recording sheet

Read top to bottom in one session. 🎧 VOICE TRACK lines are recorded here and laid over the clips; 🎤 VEO3 LIP-SYNC lines are ALSO listed for continuity but are voiced by Veo3 inside their clip — do not record them onto the track (or record as safety and mute).

BEAT 1 · THE HOOK — the runaway bride (flash-forward)
NARRATOR (VO)

शादी का मंडप सजा था, मेहमान खड़े थे — और दुल्हन… दुल्हन दौड़ रही थी। जिस लड़की की शादी शहर के सबसे अमीर घर में हो रही थी, वो अपने ही मंडप से भाग रही थी — एक गरीब डिलीवरी वाले का हाथ थामे। पर ठहरिए… ये कहानी यहाँ से नहीं, छह महीने पहले एक टिफिन के डिब्बे से शुरू हुई थी।

BEAT 2 · SIX MONTHS EARLIER — the tiffin wala
NARRATOR (VO)

छह महीने पहले। आलू — इस शहर का सबसे ईमानदार टिफिन वाला। सुबह चार बजे उठता, अपने हाथों से खाना बनाता, और हर डिब्बे के साथ थोड़ी-सी इज़्ज़त भी पहुँचाता था।

TAMATAR (shot 2.1)🎧 VOICE TRACK
भाई, तीस डिब्बे तैयार — आज तो ऑर्डर डबल है!
ALOO (shot 2.1)🎧 VOICE TRACK
मेहनत डबल है टमाटर, तो बरकत भी डबल होगी।
GAJAR (shot 2.2)🎧 VOICE TRACK
थैंक यू… आप नए टिफिन वाले हो ना?
ALOO (shot 2.2)🎧 VOICE TRACK
जी, आलू। खाना ऐसा कि माँ की याद आ जाए — गारंटी।
GAJAR (shot 2.3)🎧 VOICE TRACK
इतना तो लोग अपनों के लिए भी नहीं करते…
BEAT 3 · TWO WORLDS, ONE TAPRI — the lucky coin
NARRATOR (VO)

दिन गुज़रते गए। दो अलग-अलग दुनियाएँ एक चाय की टपरी पर मिलने लगीं। गाजर के लिए आलू की सादगी ही उसकी सबसे बड़ी दौलत थी।

GAJAR (shot 3.1)🎧 VOICE TRACK
एक बात बताओ — तुम हर किसी के लिए इतना क्यों सोचते हो?
ALOO (shot 3.1)🎧 VOICE TRACK
माँ कहती थी — नीयत साफ़ हो, तो रास्ते ख़ुद खुल जाते हैं।
सहकर्मी (भीड़) (shot 3.2)🎧 VOICE TRACK
अरे मैडम, डिलीवरी वाले से इतनी दोस्ती?
GAJAR (shot 3.2)🎧 VOICE TRACK
इंसान की पहचान कपड़ों से नहीं, नीयत से होती है।
GAJAR (shot 3.3)🎧 VOICE TRACK
ये माँ का लकी सिक्का है। अब ये तुम्हारे पास रहेगा।
ALOO (shot 3.3)🎧 VOICE TRACK
तो अब क़िस्मत भी तुम्हारी अमानत हुई, गाजर जी।
MOOLI (shot 3.4)🎧 VOICE TRACK

🎬 Shots — every 8s clip, fully self-contained

Shot number = play order. Each shot: IMAGE prompt → still (2–3 takes) → VIDEO prompt → one 8-second Veo3 clip. Character locks are already inside every prompt.

BEAT 1 · THE HOOK — the runaway bride (flash-forward) · 3 shots
NARRATOR (VO)

शादी का मंडप सजा था, मेहमान खड़े थे — और दुल्हन… दुल्हन दौड़ रही थी। जिस लड़की की शादी शहर के सबसे अमीर घर में हो रही थी, वो अपने ही मंडप से भाग रही थी — एक गरीब डिलीवरी वाले का हाथ थामे। पर ठहरिए… ये कहानी यहाँ से नहीं, छह महीने पहले एक टिफिन के डिब्बे से शुरू हुई थी।

📝 EDIT NOTE: Edit timing: hold the VO's final sentence ('पर ठहरिए… छह महीने पहले…') so it lands exactly ON the 1.3 freeze-frame; let 1.2 run under the middle sentence so the narration keeps driving through the villain shot.

SHOT 1.1 · 8s
No dialogue — narrator VO / ambience over this clip.
IMAGE PROMPT — Shot 1.1
CAMERA: wide tracking shot, low angle, running with the couple. SUBJECT — CHARACTERS IN FRAME (render each EXACTLY as described): GAJAR, the warm-hearted heroine — a photorealistic young woman whose entire head IS a single fresh CARROT (must be a real gajar/carrot). HEAD SHAPE & SKIN: a tapering conical bright red-orange carrot with fine ridge rings across the surface, and a lush crown of feathery green carrot fronds flowing back from the top like hair. FACE NOW: breathless, eyes blazing with resolve, glancing back over her shoulder; bright kind eyes and a soft mouth formed naturally in the carrot skin, a rosy glow on the cheeks. BODY & DRESS: a normal adult human body with ordinary human hands, wearing a heavy deep-red and gold bridal lehenga with gold jewellery, a sheer red dupatta pinned over her frond crown, bridal bangles and mehndi on her human hands. DO NOT: she is NOT a radish and NOT a mooli — never white, cream or pink, never a rounded bulb; and NOT a tomato and NOT a red chilli — her head stays bright red-ORANGE with its fine ridge rings, never the deep red of her clothing; keep the red-orange taper and the green frond crown always visible, even through a sheer dupatta. NEXT CHARACTER: ALOO, the humble tiffin-delivery hero — a photorealistic young man whose entire head IS a single large raw POTATO (must be a real aloo/potato). HEAD SHAPE & SKIN: a lumpy oval tuber slightly larger than a human head, matte earthy tan-brown skin with fine dimples, shallow potato eyes and a few faint soil freckles, dry matte texture, never shiny. FACE NOW: jaw set, protective, gripping her hand; warm brown eyes and a gentle mouth formed naturally in the potato skin. BODY & DRESS: a normal adult human body with ordinary human hands, wearing a simple off-white cotton kurta over worn dark jeans, a faded red-checked gamcha around his neck, a scuffed grey-blue delivery windbreaker with a boxy insulated delivery bag slung on his shoulder. DO NOT: his head is NOT a rock, NOT a coconut, NOT a smooth brown ball — a real dimpled potato; not orange, no leafy top, never shiny.
